The overall paint job was great. However if your picky about your paint, you better let them know in great detail what it is you want before they start the job. They painted over the original factory pinstripes and the chrome moldings that go around my car. It didn't ruin the car, it just doesn't have pinstripes anymore and there is no more chrome moldings. But like I said it wasn't a big deal because the paint job was great and the moldings were to old anyway. Overall, I'm satisfied. Only thing that was lacking was attention to detail.</review>

< review>
Like every apartment complex, Deerwood has its PROS & CONS

PROS: all the women in the office are extremely kind and so helpful, the community itself is well maintained, neighbors are really nice, family oriented, very safe place, has a small park with enough running space for children. The apartments here are very spacious with updated features. Everything about the apartment features are really nice. Maintenance team is so kind, and they do fix your issues but sometimes they will take up to 6 days to go to your apartment. If you have children, and love the pool, I think it‚Äôs awesome that Deerwood has a separate pool for kids. During the day it‚Äôs very quiet, and peaceful. Especially if you want to take a walk around the complex.

CONS: I had so many issues with the water temperature in the shower. No matter where you turn the knob, the water will either get extremely hot or very cold every 5-10 seconds. The office doesn‚Äôt really answer their phones all the time (I have had to call up to 8 times needing help with something) and the sad part was, when I went to the office, I saw their door open and I called again to see if they would bother picking up, and they didn‚Äôt. Parking becomes a HUGE issue after 5/6pm. You will more than likely not find a parking spot after those times unless you own a carport (only one carport comes with the lease, you‚Äôd have to pay for a second monthly). My biggest regret with living here is choosing an apartment closest to the street, Camino Del Norte. I cannot stress enough how terrible it is at night time. If you are not used to constant noise or floors/windows shaking dramatically, you will NOT sleep. When big cars or trucks pass by, your floors, and windows will shake drastically. It feels like an earthquake. It also doesn‚Äôt help that the windows make a loud noise while they shake. I have spoken to my neighbors about it, and they also experience the same, they hate it. Every family guest or friend that I had overnight complained of not getting any sleep whatsoever because of the street. <date>1423200341559<//date><response>None</response>< name>
Jen H</name>
<review>Superior sandwich.... hmm I don't know about that.

Which Wich is a catchy name just wish their sandwiches were as good as their name. I came in wanting to grab something quick before my workout and decided to give this place a try. It's sandwiched (yes, pun intended) right between Starbucks and Five Guys in a plaza with teeny tiny parking. I came in mid-afternoon so it was pretty much empty and I had all the time in the world to decide what I wanted. With their set up, I can imagine it would be a push and shove type situation to get your order in and I don't want to be all up in that.... no thanks!

So first you start off by picking the brown bag that a has a list of stuff you could possibly want in your sandwich. The brown bags are sorted out by type of meat so don't grab the wrong one! For this occasion, I went with turkey but they had a ton of other options like beef, italian, veggie, chicken, etc. After you select the brown bag, you grab one of the red sharpies and start creating your beautiful masterpiece of a sandwich. They also have specialty sandwich meat types on the top, for example, the turkey one had thank you turkey which is thanksgiving turkey which is pretty much your thanksgiving turkey meal in a sandwich or turkey reuben which comes with saurkraut and thousand island. I went ahead and picked the Thanksgiving turkey because who could pass up stuffing and cranberry sauce? not this girl! I also added lettuce, cheese, saurkraut (can't get enough of this stuff), banana peppers, and mustard all stuffed into a wheat roll. You also have the option of getting it cold or hot (but getting it hot takes longer). Once you're done with your brown bag, you hand it to the cashier and pay.

My sandwich took about 5-7 minutes, it wasn't that long since no one else was there. The workers were pretty friendly, they talked to me as I was waiting for the sandwich. When I got it, I was surprised by how big it was. I guess I thought 7" was a little smaller, so that was a happy surprise. However, I did not like how mushy my entire sandwich was. I swear, it was like 85% stuffing and then 5% cranberry sauce, and the last 10% was all the other stuff which includes turkey. Where was the turkey?!?! I ordered the Thank you turkey not thank you stuffing sandwich -_- and for a hot sandwich, it wasn't that hot either. The sandwich was underwhelming and I didn't feel like it was worth the $7. But if you're a hugeeeeeee toppings fan then this is your joint because Which Wich has a lot of choices.

If I do go back, I'll give the shake a try since that seems to be popular and not the turkey, thank you.< /review></record></dataset><record>

Covid made everything more complicated of course but I set off to find someone who could help me. I did numerous ‚Äúvirtual‚Äù appointments with several provides who all had raving reviews and advertised ‚Äúpainless‚Äù dentistry. I knew it would take a lot for me to trust and feel comfortable with anyone. Many of those I spoke with were pleasant but I still felt like they were passing judgement ‚Äì I didn‚Äôt need anyone to tell me how bad my teeth were or how ghastly they looked ‚Äì believe me I was more than aware. I had been dealing with my mouth for years and made a point to not smile with an open mouth when I sat in board meetings, interviewed clients, or even socialized. Then I met Dr. Field and that was the start of relationship that has profoundly changed my world.

From day 1, Dr. Field has been thorough, thoughtful, and compassionate. He has listened to me, heard me, and addressed all my concerns and my fears. He has given me a complete smile makeover and at times, it has been scary but he has always acknowledged my fears and made sure that any pain I was experiencing was addressed ‚Äì this is huge for me. I have a fairly high pain tolerance, but we all have our limits and research has shown that you heal faster when pain is addressed, and you are able to sleep. I am so thankful that I found Dr. Field and I still become a bit emotional when I think about how much he has improved my quality of life, how others respond to my new smile, how I no longer shy away from the camera, how much better I feel about myself and the comfort that I get knowing that my overall health is being addressed.

Being in the "high risk" group, we were very concerned about venturing out for medical and dental services.  Dr. Field's staff was wonderful in contacting us early on to re-schedule appointments that had to be canceled during the initial shutdown. We know how important dental care is to our overall health, so as the weeks went on, we knew we had to come in asap when they could once again see us.

Finally, we had appointments. I had been having concerns about two teeth;  one had just had a full crown pop off three days prior.  So I carefully gathered the things I needed to bring with me and prepared for my second venture out of the house since March.  I was nervous and had not yet adjusted to the precautions one now takes when going anywhere, including a grocery store visit I'd planned to make after my appointment, so I was feeling a bit frazzled.

Long story short, I sat down in the chair, relieved and comforted by the comprehensive safety procedures in place and how closely they were being followed. I reached into my bag for the container with the crown that had come off, only to find out it wasn't there!  I was literally shaking, wondering where I'd left it; had it fallen out as I rushed to get ready?  Anggie calmly had me get up to check my car (not there, so had to be at home), then she and Dr. Karl looked at the schedule and discussed how they could somehow fit me in that same day so I could come back with the crown, rather than wait at least a day for a new appointment.  I was so grateful and impressed that they would do this, knowing how tightly booked their schedule is.  I was back about an hour later and Dr. Karl got the crown successfully back in place.  What a relief!  I appreciated that he talked about what he was doing and why, as Dr. Field always does.

I had also broken my upper retainer, so as Anggie took the mold for a new one I had a few minutes to talk with her, and I learned just how seriously everyone in the office takes the COVID-19 precautions.  I mentioned how uncomfortable it must be to have the N95 mask on while working and talking with patients, and she told me that they put the gear on before they come into the office and only take it off when they are outside the office for a break.  I had noted to myself that everyone had the PPE on, even someone sitting in their office, where you might expect to see them take if off for a 'breather'.  The protocols for both patients and staff seemed impressively strict and thorough, yet, as always, the staff was 100% positive and helpful.  What had started out as a very stressful day, ended on such a positive note.  And I was so relieved to know that I did not have to worry about my husband coming in for his appointment the following week.

We've been patients of Peninsula Center for Cosmetic Dentistry for quite a few years - starting when I consulted Dr. Hartley about problems with my teeth, and not feeling comfortable with my dentist's continued patching of the problems, but not recognizing or fixing the underlying issue.  They have always gone 'above and beyond' in providing amazing care, even in unusual circumstances (being in a remote location with a dental emergency).

Long-winded review, but posting in the event it can help someone else having similar concerns, looking for an exceptional dental practice.</review>

Thought to myself that I should enjoy a spa and decided that this was a great place to choose. I was not disappointed. This place was wonderful.

The environment was really relaxing. The service was amazing. Everyone was nice.

Storage available to put your stuff. Showers available to wash off after.

There was a parking lot across the street that was supposed to accommodate the time spent at the spa, but the time limit seemed to pass by really quick, so expect to pay for parking.

Only downside is the place is very pricey. Hard pressed to keep coming unless I became filthy rich.< /Review>

<user_name>Daniel Massaro< /user_name>< time>
1440404593160</time>

< review>
By most people's ratings, 4.5 stars is amazing. But in this case would be an insult.
Every detail in this spa was catered to and executed with absolute consciousness & conviction.
From the moment I stepped into the main door, being greeted by a warm smile while simultaneously experiencing an injection of soothing fragrances and soft traditional music i was sold.
And then being taken back through the double doors was something i did not expect. An extremely clean, long, beautiful, minimalistic and traditional dimly lit hallway.
I was sat down in the lounge, my shoes removed and seated into an incredibly comfortable couch. An attendant served traditional green tea, Iced tea, iced water, and a chilled jell-o like dessert. The experience of relaxation had begun long before entering the actual massage room.
I was then introduced to Piku (sorry if i misspelled it), a lovely lady who's skills are beyond measure and had me feeling like royalty. I have to be honest that my expectation was already set really high the moment I walked into the spa. But it was perfectly matched with the pleasant and carefully selected therapist.
For those that may find the price a little above average, just remember this place and service IS above average. You actually get MORE than what you could expect. It's a complete experience. One that I will often frequent when in the Los Angeles area.
Treat yourself RIGHT; reward yourself to something real instead of guessing what kind of therapist or experience you will get. Can't wait for my upcoming session.
Domo arigato Team Tomoko!

- Daniel</review>
